Important News Two

North China to Hold Water Conservancy Discussion Conference 78

Scheduled to Open on April 1st for One Week

Tianjin Correspondence: The North China Water Conservancy Commission, whose jurisdiction reaches several provinces in North China, is responsible for matters such as river management, water conservancy, and disaster prevention. However, the vastness of the land often makes it difficult to implement plans. During the sixth general meeting in October of last year, it was decided to convene a North China Water Conservancy Discussion Conference in April of this year to discuss water conservancy construction issues in various parts of North China, and to formulate procedures for various water conservancy facilities that should be implemented. The conference will also exchange the latest theories and experiences on water conservancy projects, bringing experts together to facilitate water conservancy construction. Since the approval of this case, the Water Conservancy Commission has been preparing for the progress of the discussion conference. Recently, the general plan has been finalized and submitted to the Construction Committee for approval and record. It is reported that the scope of discussion is quite broad. All construction departments and responsible officials and senior technicians of river management agencies in Henan, Hebei, the three northeastern provinces, Rehe, Chahar, Suiyuan, Shaanxi, Gansu, and Shanxi provinces are invited. For the sake of collective wisdom, representatives from the Yangtze River and Huai River Water Conservancy Commissions are also invited to participate. All those who have handled water conservancy construction in North China and have achieved results, or who have works and inventions in water conservancy academics, regardless of whether they have a position or not, are also solicited and invited. Letters are also sent to various water conservancy agencies and factories at home and abroad, asking them to send plans, charts, statistical reports, water conservancy books, engineering instruments, engineering machinery, and other water conservancy materials that can be used for observation to the commission as much as possible, taking the opportunity to open a water conservancy exhibition, publicly exhibit them, in order to popularize water conservancy knowledge. The officers of the discussion conference have now been determined, with Zhang Jingjiang as the chairman, honorary chairmen Li Shizeng, Xu Yongchang, and Cui Tingxian, and vice chairman Zeng Yangfu. The honorary vice chairmen are the directors of the construction departments of each province, the presidium is the members of the North China Water Conservancy Commission, and the opening chairman is Chen Maojie, the chairman of the North China Water Conservancy Association. The opening date is from April 1st, for a total of seven days.

All Circles in Northeast Celebrate Panchen Lama's Birthday 79

Shenyang Correspondence: The Panchen Lama, not tolerated by the Mongolian party, came to Shenyang to reside, and has been there for several months. The 10th (the twelfth day of the first month of the lunar calendar) was his 50th birthday. All circles in Liaoning and Ningxia specially organized a Public Birthday Celebration Committee and held a public celebration ceremony at the Provincial Education Association (the old site of the Imperial Palace) on the 11th. On that day, the authorities, in order to show their congratulations to all merchants and citizens, specially informed all shops to hang flags for one day. The entrance of the Education Association was decorated with a yellow cloth and colored arch. From 9 a.m. to 12 p.m., the highest authorities in the Northeast, such as the Political Affairs Committee, the Border Defense Command, the Provincial Government, and senior and mid-level dignitaries from military, political, academic circles, all gathered at the association. At 10:45 a.m., the Panchen Lama, accompanied by translator Zhang Yuliang, secretary Liu Rongguang, master of ceremonies Xia Sangdeng, and various princes and followers, traveled in six cars from the Imperial Temple. At that time, Yang Zhengzhi (deputy officer of the Border Department), Zimingzhen (head of the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau), Wang Jiarui (county magistrate of Shenyang), Wang Huayi (chairman of the Liaoning Provincial Education Association) and a group of dozens of people greeted him at the front gate. At 1 p.m., the Panchen Lama took a specially prepared yellow car, with the Kuomintang emblem painted on the front of the car. Amidst the melodious military music, he alighted from the car and was led by the welcomers to the Education Association Tongzhi Hall, and then turned to Baoke Palace to rest. The Panchen Lama wore a scattered flower yellow satin robe, purplish-brown patterned satin pants, a sable hat, and yellow leather boots. He then went to the Diguang Hall to hold the public celebration ceremony. In the auditorium, there was a seat for the Buddha, a yellow carpet on the ground, and satin chair covers embroidered with colorful longevity characters. On both sides hung satin couplets saying, "Fame, profit, great joy; fortune, longevity, much virtue." In the middle hung a plaque presented by Zhang Xueliang, inscribed with the four characters "Eternal Abode of the Dharmakaya," the upper inscription being "Grand Celebration of the Birthday of the Panchen Lama National Teacher" and the lower inscription "So-and-so Celebration." After the ceremony, he took a photo in front of the Wensu Pavilion. After the photo was taken, the Panchen Lama gave a speech, which was translated into Chinese, roughly saying that since the Panchen Lama came to China from Tibet in the twelfth year of the Republic of China, although he had a motherland to return to, he still had no fixed residence. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the late Great Marshal benefited the distant people, maintained Buddhism, and ordered him to come east, caring for him in every way, so that he had something to rely on. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, Commander-in-Chief Zhang Hanqing cared even more for the Panchen Lama, and the monks and Tibetans who followed the Panchen Lama, the military, political, and civilian officials of the four northeastern provinces. At a time when the finances of Liaoning Province were stretched, they arranged monthly allowances to help the distressed. The Panchen Lama was deeply grateful. Today, on the Panchen Lama's birthday, Commander-in-Chief Zhang, the Provincial Government Chairman Zang, and all civil and military officials, legal entities, and gentlemen, disregarding the Spring Festival celebrations and busy political affairs, showed sincerity and love, gathered to celebrate, and in addition to accepting this honor, he was endlessly grateful. Although the Panchen Lama is the leader of the Yellow Sect, he is only passing on the mantle of the Buddha, and has not left his physical body. Since he came to Liaoning, he has experienced four years of assistance from the officials and people of the four northeastern provinces. The officials and people of the four northeastern provinces have become even more fond of the Panchen Lama. What virtue and ability does the Panchen Lama have to inspire such a response? This is all due to Commander-in-Chief Zhang's enthusiasm for national affairs, concern for Tibetan soil, love for distant people, and support for the true religion, which has led to this. In the future, the Panchen Lama should pray to the Buddha even more, advocate peace, and offer his humble opinion. He respectfully wishes Commander-in-Chief Zhang ten thousand years, the Provincial Chairman ten thousand years, the officials and people of the four provinces ten thousand years, and the Republic of China ten thousand years. After the speech, the Chairman of Rehe Province, Tang Yulin, the Chairman of Liaoning Province, Zang Shiyi, and the Vice Chairman of the Northeast Political Affairs Council, Yuan Jinkai, and the Director of the Liaoning Civil Affairs Department, Chen Wenxue, accompanied the Panchen Lama to the Jiayin Hall to watch a play. At about 3 p.m., a banquet was held for the Panchen Lama at the Baoke Palace. After the banquet, Tang, Zang, and Yuan bid farewell one after another. Chen accompanied the Panchen Lama back to the Jiayin Hall to watch a play. The plays included "Great Blessing," "Boundless Longevity," "Prosperous Spring and Autumn," "Qingdingzhu," and "Meeting of Heroes." At 4:20 p.m., the guests sent the Panchen Lama off the stage, and the director of the Panchen Lama Reception Office, Li Shaobai, personally escorted the Panchen Lama to his residence. At about 6 p.m., the guests dispersed. This afternoon at 3 p.m., the Panchen Lama will host a banquet for all circles at the Education Association. (February 12th)

Ardent Anti-Japanese Movement of Koreans 80

Korean Students in Longjing Village Hold Demonstration

Shenyang Correspondence: The Korean anti-Japanese movement has been extremely vigorous and passionate. There is no doubt about it in the major cities of Korea. Even in Longjing Village, a demonstration was held on the 5th of this month. Although the Japanese police forcibly suppressed it and treated them in every way, the patriotic spirit of the Korean youth was not slightly subdued. The following is the situation described by witnesses in the area:

Since the outbreak of student unrest in Korea, the Japanese police have been under special martial law. They frequently searched Korean hotels and private schools. In recent days, more than 250 Koreans have been detained by the Japanese police at the consulate, mostly students, but there is no concrete evidence of their crimes. At noon on the 5th, more than 100 Japanese consulate police officers, all fully armed, either on horseback or on foot, went in groups of three or five to Korean student dormitories and the Dacheng Middle School to conduct searches, and forced the students to go to the consulate. The students had no weapons and were unable to resist, so they obeyed. Unexpectedly, in front of the consulate, a Japanese policeman pushed a Korean student down and kicked his head with force, causing him to bleed profusely and faint immediately. When the Japanese police saw that he was about to die, they carried him into the prison. The rest were also forced into the prison. When the students were forced to go to the consulate, they were in excellent spirits and kept shouting "Korean Independence Forever."

At about 1 p.m. on the 5th, Korean students in Longjing Village held a demonstration. The Japanese police surrounded and arrested them, arresting a total of 57 students. When they rushed into the consulate, there were four Korean women, some carrying children on their backs, behind the students, also shouting "Korea Forever," and were arrested by the Japanese police and taken to the consulate.

At about 2 p.m. on the 5th, on the main street near the Japanese consulate, a Japanese policeman, riding a tall horse with a rope tied to it, tied a Korean student (about seventeen or eighteen years old) by two of his fingers and galloped along the street. The student had no choice but to run after him. However, how could a person's running speed catch up with a galloping horse? The two thumbs were tightly bound by the rope, and the pain was indescribable. Yet he still shouted "Long Live."

At about 4 p.m. on the 5th, more than a dozen Japanese policemen patrolled on horseback, galloping through the streets. All Korean private schools were searched. Later, behind the Dongshan Entu School, eight youths were arrested, including one woman. In front of the Korean bank, a student from the Dongxing School was arrested and taken to the Japanese Consulate General for detention. (February 12th)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang 81

The Construction Committee Sends Commissioners to Investigate the Electricity Industry. The Construction Committee believes that the privately-operated electrical businesses in various places urgently need investigation in order to improve them. It is reported that it has sent Commissioner Zhang Baotong, and the Construction Department has also sent Technician Jin Pu, to inspect various places. The county government has already been notified by letter. In addition to notifying the electrical business authorities, County Magistrate Jin has also separately forwarded the notification to his subordinates for protection.

The County Government Summons Local Chiefs to Instruct Them. In this county, the harvest of grain rentals in the southern townships last winter was only 30-40%, which affected the national tax revenue and caused a sharp reduction. The grain transport was originally based on past precedents, with the lunar New Year's Eve as the initial deadline. However, most of it was not moved last year. The county government and the Finance Bureau jointly presented a request to the Finance Department to extend the deadline by half a month and strictly urge rent collection. The county government specially summoned the local chiefs of each district on the 17th to listen to the instructions. The general instructions were that the grain transport has been approved for an extension of half a month, with the deadline being the 20th. All industries should be notified to pay within the deadline. The public silver from last year should be closed out at the end of this month, and all chiefs should be ordered to pay the full amount, without any shortage. All tenants should be notified to quickly return the rent to avoid being pursued for payment.

Suzhou 82

Han Jin's Steaming Bone Examination. The case of Jin, the daughter-in-law of the late Qing official Han Qipangzi, who resided at No. 30 Gejia Lane, Changmen Nei, who died under unclear circumstances, has been lingering for more than a year. Now, her relatives Han Guoduo and Han Guolin have come forward to report it, accusing the悍servant Shi Junqing and others of murdering her. After accepting the case, the Wuxian District Court detained Shi Junqing and Li Chenshi. Yesterday (the 17th) morning, at the temple east of the Jiezhuang Temple in Xiyuan outside Changmen, Han Jin's body was exhumed and steamed bones were examined. A shed was pre-built for steaming the bones. The inspection officers of Zhenjiang and Wujiang counties were invited to Suzhou to assist. The president of Boxi Hospital, Li Guangxun, and others were invited to help with the examination. On that day, Inspector Lai led the police to preside over the inspection. At 2 p.m., Han Jin's coffin was carried to the corpse field. First, the deceased's husband Han Youjiu and the plaintiff Han Guoduo and others made a written statement before the coffin was opened, and then the coffin was opened, the corpse was taken out, the clothes were cut off, and the whole body was washed. Because the corpse had not completely rotted, it could still be examined. Silver needles were then inserted into the mouth and anus, and taken out after about ten minutes, and no traces of poison were found. The whole body was then covered with distiller's grains, and silver needles were still inserted into the mouth and anus. Cotton was then used to cover the body for testing. The examination was completed at 6 p.m., but no traces of injury were found. It was then wrapped in cotton wool and placed back in the original coffin, which was then sealed. It has not yet been decided whether to use steamed bones for the examination today (the 18th).

Granting a Ten-Day Extension for Grain and Labor Tax. The Wuxian Finance Bureau set up a counter to collect the 18th year's lower season labor silver and grain rice. According to regulations, the deadline was the 17th, and today (the 18th) a late payment penalty of 20% will be charged. The County Government has now approved the request of the Tianye Association to extend the deadline for one month, and approved the extension for ten days.

Provincial Government Arbitrates Garment Industry Dispute. The labor and management sides of the garment industry in Suzhou had a dispute over various issues such as hiring employees and salaries, which has lasted for half a year and has not been resolved. Both parties have requested assistance from the provincial government. The provincial government has already organized an arbitration committee and summoned representatives from both labor and management to the province for arbitration. The labor side has now appointed Sheng Zhixing and others as plenipotentiary representatives, and they went to the province on the 17th, but the management side is still hesitating.

County Bonds Replaced by Treasury Bonds. The fourth lottery for the return of capital on Wuxian military bonds has been held. However, due to the county government being ordered to raise funds for the staffing reduction treasury bonds, the winning bonds of 150,000 yuan were converted into staffing reduction treasury bonds. However, the conversion method has not yet been decided, so the Bond Committee convened a meeting on the 17th, and it was resolved that the bonus of two yuan per hundred yuan of the staffing reduction treasury bonds would be granted, and interest would be calculated from January. As for the date of encashment, it will be determined after the treasury bonds are received. Interest on the non-winning bonds will be paid from March 1.

Qingpu 84

Girl's Elopement Results in Negotiations. A daughter of Pu of a certain town in Qingpu, named Yuexian, is already of marriageable age. Last year, she was betrothed to a son of Zhang of this town through a matchmaker. Unexpectedly, Yuexian recently fell in love with a certain Jia, an employee of a certain organization, and eloped without a trace the day before yesterday. When Pu noticed, she had already disappeared and was nowhere to be found. It is said that Zhang has invited the original matchmaker to have a major negotiation with Pu, but it is not known how this matter will be resolved.

Gambling Failure Leads to Son Punching His Elderly Mother. Wu Qian, an elderly woman from outside the West Gate of this county, is in her sixties. Her son, named Baosheng, earns a living as a laborer. During the lunar New Year, he entered the gambling house and lost all his remaining money, and pawned his clothes to make a final bet, and then returned home empty-handed. He asked his mother for money, but Wu Qian sternly refused. Baosheng then punched his elderly mother, but fortunately Zheng Ju dissuaded him, and she was not injured.

Meningitis Discovered in Zhujie Pavilion. Since the beginning of spring, meningitis has been prevalent in Zhujie Pavilion Town in Qingpu, and three people have already died. Most of the patients are young children, and they often die within three or four hours.

Wuxi 85

Qingcheng City Black Night Vendetta Melee: In Wei Jiatang, the 15th district of this county (Qingcheng City), around 10 o'clock the night before last, a group of fifty or sixty burly men suddenly arrived, speaking in local accents and wielding flashlights, wooden sticks, and other weapons. They made a lot of noise in the area and started fires along the street. They then knocked on doors one by one. The villagers, who were already asleep, were startled awake by the knocking. Suspecting a robbery, they dared not open their doors. Some of the braver ones sounded gongs to gather the crowd and resist, resulting in two villagers being injured by the burly men. As the villagers gathered in greater numbers, they captured a burly man named Liu Tingquan on the spot and handed him over to the 15th District Office. The remaining burly men fled in panic. Afterwards, after questioning by District Chief Yuan, Liu Tingquan claimed that he was only seeking revenge.

Collection of Fees: The township chiefs and deputy chiefs of the 1st District Office, due to the lack of funding, held a meeting and decided to collect feast donation fees to be used as autonomous funds. The County Education Bureau has also started to handle the matter, and the county government recently submitted the situation to the Education Department for review. Yesterday, they received instructions to properly formulate a plan and submit it for approval. Lu Renshou, the director of the County Education Bureau, had previously made a trip to the provincial capital. The day before yesterday, the township chiefs and deputy chiefs also sent representatives Xuan Junhou, Qian Nianxiu, and Cheng Yuming to the provincial capital to petition, which was very successful. Yesterday, they returned to Wuxi from the provincial capital.

Theft Case in Wu Jiangxiang: Wu Huifeng, a resident of Wu Jiangxiang, 596th Tu, 2nd District (Jingyun City), (currently serving as a meritorious administrator at the 2nd District Office), is from a family of modest means. Unexpectedly, around 10 o'clock the night before last, six robbers suddenly arrived, wielding a Mauser pistol, two handguns, wooden sticks, flashlights, and other items. They broke into the house, dragged Wu Huifeng from his bed, tied him up with rope, and searched the house at will. After an hour, they fled with their loot. Upon inspection, the stolen items included 60 silver dollars, four small silver coins, two gold rings, one gold hair clasp, two gold Ruyi ornaments, one gold ear pick, one silver watch, and clothing, totaling an estimated loss of over 300 dollars.

Tragedy of a Traveler Jumping from a Building at the New World Hotel: In room 42 of the New World Hotel on Tongyun Road, Wuxi, there were six or seven travelers, including Wang Bingkui, Zhang Renbao, and Xu A'er. On the evening of the 16th, someone secretly reported to the military inspection office in the Wuxi garrison that there were several reactionary elements secretly meeting in room 42 of the hotel. They requested that soldiers be dispatched to investigate and arrest them. Nie Shaowen, the director of the inspection office, upon receiving the report, immediately dispatched inspector Chu Ziming with several soldiers to search the room. Finding the door tightly closed, they knocked on it. Hearing a hubbub of voices inside, the inspector became even more suspicious and cocked his gun. Hearing the sound of the gun being cocked outside the door, Xu A'er and Zhang Renbao panicked and jumped out of the window, falling into a small alley next to the hotel. Both were seriously injured. At that time, Wang and the others had no choice but to open the door. After Chu and his men inquired about the situation and conducted a brief search, they returned to the garrison and reported to Director Nie that they were not reactionary elements. After jumping from the building, both Xu A'er and Zhang Renbao collapsed on the ground. Xu A'er suffered a head injury, and blood flowed like a river. His waist was also seriously injured. Zhang Renbao injured his arm. Later, friends hired rickshaws to take them to Tongren Hospital for treatment.

Changzhou 86

County Court Established: Wu Zengshan, the acting president of the Wujin County Court, and Xu Heling, the chief prosecutor, along with court clerks, went to the county government around 1:00 PM on the 16th to take over the establishment of the court and make a public announcement. It is learned that the appointed staff, in addition to the previously arrived court clerk Ling Chen, also include court clerks Xu Mingzhen and Wang Boyuan, and record clerks Tai Zhenya and Zhang Zhonglin.

Dalen Yarn Factory Transferred: Wujin Dalen Yarns Weaving Factory was transferred to the newly organized Dacheng Company because the shareholders had no intention of operating it. Liu Guojun came forward to take over. The Shanghai board of directors of Dalen specially sent factory director Hu Wenqin and representatives Chen Dazai and two others (three people in total) yesterday (the 16th) to Changzhou to handle the handover. The procedures have all been completed. The employees and workers raised requests for severance pay and bonuses. Representatives of the old company believed that it could be discussed and handled within a possible scope. If the difference was too large, they would ask to send representatives to Shanghai to negotiate. On the morning of the 17th, the county party headquarters specially convened a discussion between both parties to resolve everything.

Jiangyin 87

Puhui Bridge Inspection of Male Corpse: A young man's body, killed by gunfire, was found west of Puhui Bridge. After the Public Security Bureau reported to the county for inspection, it was learned that the deceased was named Tan Wuguan, from Xia Siwei Port, Jingjiang, 30 years old. He worked at Lao Renji Scissors Shop near Wei Guan Archway in Wuxi. On the 10th of this month, he went from Wuxi to Jiangyin to Jingjiang. After arriving home on the 14th, he crossed the river. After lingering at Zhu Tailor's house for a moment, he turned around and went out. He did not return until night. After inspection by Coroner Tong, there was a gunshot wound at the base of the ear, exiting from the mouth, blowing off both hands. There was a photo shadow. Beside him was a certificate from the 3rd section fire brigade of the Central District of Wuxi. After the inspection, the body was collected by the Beiwai Fire Brigade. On the afternoon of the 15th, his father, Tan Shaopei, came to Jiangyin after hearing the news to take care of everything and requested the county government to arrest the murderer.

Lu Family Robbed, One Thief Captured: The Lu Baolin family in Zhouzhuang was robbed on the 13th by seven bandits, three as lookouts and four entering to rob. While the robbers were searching, they were suddenly discovered by Baolin's son, who mobilized the villagers. They captured one bandit, Wang Baosheng, on the spot, and the Zhouzhuang Security Corps handed him over to the county government for interrogation. He denied being a thief, saying, "I live in the Zou area, 9th Tu, Hengjing past Shichuang, Xumen, Suzhou. I had business with Yuan Songmao's family, and was arrested on the way," etc. After interrogation, he was taken into custody.

Zhenjiang 88

Planning to Dredge Zhangfu Canal: Northern Jiangsu has suffered frequent droughts for years, and the counties of Huai'an and Yangzhou have been particularly affected. The reason for this is that the source of the Xiangyun Canal is not smooth. The floodwaters of the Yi and Si rivers are insufficient, and the Huai River cannot be diverted into the Yun River due to the Zhangfu River. This results in drought nine years out of ten, and the people's lives are unbearable. The people of various counties have gathered to discuss dredging the Zhangfu River to irrigate farmland and take care of transportation. This measure will be beneficial to the management of the Yun River. Representatives from various counties have gathered in the provincial capital to discuss the implementation methods. The office is located at the Fengshen Temple on the riverside.

Judicial Officials Promoted and Noted: Feng Shide, the presiding judge of the criminal division of the Zhenjiang Chi Fang Court, has been transferred to Shanghai Provisional Court as a judge of the civil division. Court clerk Shen Ying has also been transferred to Shanghai Provisional Court as the director of administrative affairs. In addition, Zhou Baochu, a candidate judge, has been transferred from the Jiangsu Higher Court to the Wujin County Court as a full judge. Record clerk Peng Ruisheng has been transferred to the same court as a student clerk.

Chamber of Commerce Requests Smooth Transportation of Goods: The Zhenjiang Chamber of Commerce reported that since the opening of the Pingpu Railway, there have been very few freight cars. Merchants' goods along the line cannot be transported, and have been piling up for a long time, causing financial stagnation and deterioration of goods. Merchants are suffering immeasurable losses. Yesterday, a telegram was sent to the Ministry of Railways requesting that measures be taken to facilitate transportation, either by adding freight cars daily or by borrowing vehicles from other lines, so that all the goods piled up along the line can be transported out, benefiting both national economy and people's livelihood.

Detective Team Uncovers Serial Bandit: Wang Jinghua and other members of the detective team of the Jiangsu Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau yesterday arrested serial bandit Da Fenghuang and kidnapper Wang Yanfu, as well as harboring criminals Miao Yinshi and Xu Yinshi, in a certain place in the city. They also rescued a three-year-old boy, Gong, from the Daqiao area who had been kidnapped. After being questioned, bandit Da confessed to robbing the homes of Min Keren, Qian Xihua, Bai Baishan, Chuan Baishi, and others in the city, as well as kidnapping the Gong boy from Daqiao. Wang Yanfu, Miao Yinshi, Xu Yinshi, and others also confessed to kidnapping the Gong boy and harboring him. After the confession, Captain Peng planned to escort the criminals to the Provincial Public Security Bureau for legal proceedings today.

P Yangzhou

266th Regiment Stationed in Gaobao: The headquarters of the 133rd Brigade stationed in Yangzhou has dispatched the 266th Regiment to Gaobao and other places for garrison duty. They have been transported north on civilian boats over the past two days (the 16th), using small steamers from companies such as Dada and Fuyun.

Education Association Executive Committee Case: The County Education Association held its 22nd Executive Committee meeting yesterday. The resolutions included: (1) Candidates for the successor of the Education Director: (A) Supervising and guiding the current director; (B) Issuing a declaration stating the importance of the candidate, and that there should be no cyclical appointments; (C) Reporting the shortcomings of those who are plotting to succeed; (D) The successor must be fair and honest. (2) Sending a letter to Director Ling, requesting that he announce the relief items from previous terms before leaving office. (3) Submitting a report to the Provincial Director, stating that the supervisor has shown no achievements or integrity since taking office, and requesting that another person be appointed. (4) Primary school students: free of charge; high school students: levy appropriately; junior high school tuition: charge as usual; and oppose the use of tuition to offset regular expenses, submitting a petition to the Provincial Party Department, Education Department, and County Government to order the bureau to implement it. (5) The best graduates of Gu Elementary School will be sent up one person, with free admission for impoverished students and fees for the rest, starting from the first semester of the 19th year. (6) Submitting a report to the Provincial Education Bureau and the County Education Bureau, earnestly implementing equal treatment for urban and rural schools.

Handling Civil Oath Registration: The Jiangdu County Government received an order from the Provincial Department yesterday, stating that township citizens must take an oath and register according to regulations in order to have the right to attend township citizen's congresses and exercise the four powers. The order instructed them to quickly handle the registration. It is reported that after receiving the order, the County Government has forwarded instructions to the district offices to quickly handle the civil oath registration matters in townships according to the previously issued rules.

Qingjiang 89

Huaxing Pawnshop Labor Dispute: The Huaxing Pawnshop in this port has been withdrawing capital by various shareholders over the years, leading to poor turnover and declining business. Therefore, this month, they dismissed the middle counter staff and small heads, including Kang Dekui. After being dismissed, Kang did not bring all of his belongings out. At 11 a.m., Kang went to the pawnshop to retrieve his belongings, accompanied by a small attendant named Shen. Unexpectedly, Zhou, the pawnshop's accountant, refused. Kang then reported the matter to the other 24 small attendants in the pawnshop, who negotiated with manager Li Maoru as a group, demanding 870 yuan in customary dismissal pay. Knowing that he could not stop them, Li first requested the Chamber of Commerce to mediate, and then requested the County Government to send political police to suppress them. The County Party Headquarters also sent a special commissioner to mediate. The pawnshop authorities refused to pay a penny. On the afternoon of the 12th, at 5 p.m., Police Chief Yang Tie, acting on the County Government's order, arrested Kang Dekui and sent him to the County Government, while also comforting the other small attendants, hoping that they would settle the matter. This matter is still difficult to resolve.

Changes in Siyang and Huai'an Prison Wardens: Yang Benhui, the prison warden and detention center director of Siyang, was dismissed by the Jiangsu Higher Court due to an incident. The vacancy was filled by Li Zichen, the prison warden of Huai'an, who was appointed by the Higher Court and also served as the director of the Siyang Detention Center. Li has been transferred to take office. On the Huai'an side, Zhu Bao, the prison warden of Rugao, was ordered by the Higher Court to replace him. Zhu came to Pu on the 12th and took over the government affairs at the county government at 10 a.m. the next morning.

They were captured by the Fengjing Security Corps in November of last year and transferred to the County Court, where they were shackled and detained. Ratio of Zhejiang's Education Fees to Administrative Fees 97

The Zhejiang Education Department reported to the Ministry of Education that the total amount of various administrative fees in Zhejiang Province is 9,283,750 yuan, and the total amount of education funding in Zhejiang Province is 2,951,126 yuan. The ratio of the total amount of various administrative fees in Zhejiang Province to the total amount of education funding in Zhejiang Province is approximately 3.28 to 1.

Recent Developments in Jiangsu's Compulsory Education Office 98

The joint office for the preparation of compulsory education in various counties of Jiangsu has been established for two years, and its work has been quite diligent. It is reported that the office's periodical publications include: 1. Local Education Monthly, which provides practical teaching materials and methods for local education based on the principles of life as education and society as school, and the spirit of combining school and community, with sales of nearly 20,000 copies; 2. Special Issue on Popular Education, which is an expansion of the Special Issue on Compulsory Education, with a special column in the Central Daily News, publishing articles and methods on popular education on a regular basis, and disseminating news on popular education; The non-periodical publication is called Local Education Series, which is a collection of various individual books focusing on practical contributions to individual issues in education, including Compulsory Education Outline and Q&A on Children's Life Education (five types). Regarding experimental education, a special agreement has been made with Jiangning Yaohuamen Elementary School, Jiangdu Wangjialou Elementary School, and Baoshan Yuepu Elementary School for on-site experiments, and the results are published in the Local Education Monthly. The busiest work currently is the attached teacher correspondence department, which has 1,042 students, scattered in various counties, with over 120 lectures. As for the investigation work, there is a compulsory education investigation department, which pays special attention to teachers, economy, children, and domestic and foreign reference materials, all of which are listed in statistics as a reference for promoting compulsory education. The above is the work that the office has already done. In addition, those currently being planned and carried out include the establishment of an education center and rural improvement experimental zone near the provincial area, aiming to unite the people of the area through the power of education and jointly seek the improvement of the area's economy, autonomy, and culture. The second is the teacher referral department, which investigates teachers in various counties waiting to be hired and refers them on their behalf. In addition to allowing ordinary teachers to have considerable opportunities to develop their talents, it also hopes that excellent teachers will be distributed in various counties and benefit from adjustments and promotions. It is also heard that a large-scale local education workshop will be held in the summer of this year to allow teachers from various counties to learn from each other, and a compulsory education achievement exhibition will be held in the autumn to collect charts, statistics, films, reports, plans, and works on compulsory education from various counties for exhibition and viewing.

Local News

Education Bureau Orders Various Bookstores 99

Textbooks Should Record Departmental Orders and Mark Them Clearly

The Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to various bookstores in the city yesterday, stating, "The Ministry of Education's order No. 134 states that the wording on the covers of various textbooks published in bookstores is extremely complex, with many errors and inevitable confusion. The six items previously stipulated by the Ministry of Education must be followed and corrected. Later, the Shanghai Bookstore Association submitted a request for a flexible handling method, which was rejected. However, many of the books published in bookstores still do not follow the regulations and clearly mark the wording on the cover, which is extremely inappropriate. Therefore, in addition to issuing separate orders, this order is issued to reiterate that all textbooks published by various bookstores in the future must strictly abide by the regulations of the previous order and must not delay any further, which is extremely important." Therefore, the points that should be marked clearly on the cover of textbooks were previously stipulated by the Ministry of Education and have been relayed to the bookstores for compliance. Now, in accordance with the previous reason, in addition to issuing separate orders, this order is issued to reiterate that the bookstores must comply and must not delay any further.

Municipal Education Bureau Orders Bookstores to Submit Anti-Drug Textbooks for Compilation 100

The Municipal Education Bureau yesterday ordered various bookstores to forward the Ministry of Education's approval of the Tobacco Prohibition Association's consultation requesting that anti-drug teaching materials be added to textbooks for primary and secondary schools to various bookstores, and to submit the primary and secondary school textbooks in which anti-drug teaching materials have been incorporated to the bureau for compilation and forwarding to the Ministry of Education.

Yesterday, West Qing Won Against Qing Guang 108

Result: 40 to 26

There Were Also Three Group B Matches

Yesterday's match between Qing Guang and West Qing concerned the future of this year's Shanghai Basketball Association Group A Championship. If Qing Guang were to win, the championship would also belong to them. As a result of the competition, Qing Guang suffered a major blow and returned in defeat. West Qing is therefore closer to the championship. West Qing's victory was due to the equal strength of its internal and external players, coupled with accurate shooting and tall, fast-moving players. As a result, Qing Guang was controlled by them and allowed them to invade. Although there were famous generals who rose up to resist, most of their companions did not fulfill their duties. A single tree cannot support a collapsing building. The Qing Guang team lost to West Qing with a score of 26 to 40. Not long after the start of the battle, West Qing's Smith missed a free throw. Sullivan seized the opportunity and threw the ball with both hands, scoring a goal. Smith added two more points, making it 4-0 in the lead. At that time, Qing Guang launched a major counterattack, Tan roamed freely under the West Qing basket, throwing repeatedly, but none hit the mark. The ball then turned back. Before you knew it, West Qing added two more balls. Qing Guang's Li Baojun took advantage of the unpreparedness of others and went deep alone, causing the enemy to be at a loss and breaking the line. He jumped and threw to win the ball. West Qing's cavalry emerged one after another, and the momentum was smooth. Before long, they led 12-2. Qing Guang fought again. Tan single-handedly scored five points, while West Qing's Hennis and others also gained something. The score at halftime was West Qing 17, Qing Guang 7. After switching sides and fighting again, one of Tan's shots circled the iron ring several times and still jumped out. At this point, if there were celestial numbers, Li Sunneiwei successively added three points, and the momentum gradually grew stronger. However, West Qing's center Hennis stood tall and straight, dribbling the ball in the center, and doing whatever he wanted, causing Qing Guang to suffer a great loss. The shooting skills of their five players were indeed remarkable, so they ultimately won 40-26. From now on, West Qing's only strong opponent will be East-West. If East-West can defeat West Qing, then East-West and Qing Guang, West Qing will be divided into three parts, and who will win the championship, or another struggle will be needed. Referee Zhang Guoxun, inspector Xu Zhendong.

Yesterday's Shih Shih Football Championship

First Cycle: Each of the Three Newspapers Wins Once

The Championship Depends on Another Effort

The football championship held by the Newspaper Industry Union is divided into three teams, namely *Xin Wen Bao*, *Shen Bao*, and *Shih Shih Hsin Bao*. A double round-robin system is adopted. Yesterday, they sent a telegram to Wu Yunrui, director of the Department of Physical Education at Nanjing Central University, a bachelor of physical education and a master of education from Springfield College in the United States, asking him to take on this position. It is now heard that Mr. Wu has replied to Anhui by telegram, expressing his willingness to serve.

My Recollections on This Divisional Tournament (Part 2) by Li Huitang 114

Regarding the referees this time: The referees have been mentioned. People are probably wondering if I must have failed and am blaming others. In fact, after the game, the word "referee" should not be mentioned again. However, the referees this time have had a huge impact on us, so I have to take this opportunity to make public to the country all kinds of things about the referees this time.

Before talking about other things, I want to declare first that I dare not say that our failure this time was the fault of the referees, and I did not say that they were biased. I remember that someone in the press once comforted me very warmly, saying that if the referee for your game this time was a foreigner or someone who was a little more fair, you probably wouldn't have failed. I am very grateful for his sincerity in comforting me, but I do not quite agree with his argument.

But while I believe that he was not biased, I do have a few points of dissatisfaction with him. All three of our games this time were refereed by Mr. Ye Jiugao alone. In the first game, the opponent's center-back frequently used violence against me, wanting to injure me as soon as possible. I dare to believe that his intention was no better than that of any player in the North China-East China team. His actions were more rude than anyone else's. Mr. Ye did not warn him, but often said to me, "Ignore him."

In the second game, the originally scheduled 90 minutes passed, and there were 12 more minutes. According to Mr. Ye, it was because the players were substituted during the game to make up for the lost time. The goal that allowed the South China team to turn defeat into a draw happened to be kicked in the last two minutes. After the draw, the game should have been extended as in the first game, but Mr. Ye said that it was too late and could not continue, so the South China team, which was running out of strength, was spared from defeat. I will not discuss whether Mr. Ye's views and reasons for overtime are appropriate or not. However, once, when our left wing was attacking fiercely with the ball, Mr. Ye suddenly blew the whistle. It turned out that a center-back in the South China team had fallen to the ground due to an injury, so he stopped the game. Mr. Ye is a referee hired by the Hong Kong Association. It is really puzzling that he stopped the game when he should not have stopped the game. If Mr. Ye thinks that the game should be stopped, then next time we encounter an enemy attack, we only need one person to fake an injury and lie on the ground to get out of trouble.

Special Article

Qu's Character Indexing Method Original Author Qu Chongfu 115

Since I was a child, I attended foreign language schools. After graduating from St. John's in 1923, I went to study in the United States and did not have the opportunity to get close to Chinese dictionaries, nor did I have any research on Chinese primary schools. However, I suddenly thought that I wanted to improve Chinese dictionaries, wanting to replace the methods used in China for thousands of years with my own opinions. When you think about it, isn't this (shocking)? Isn't this (unbelievable)? Although this is the case, we all know that people in the world cannot fully predict the affairs of the world. If people in the world could fully predict the affairs of the world, then the word "hope" could be removed from all dictionaries in the world. I began to study this unpopular issue because I was impressed by the convenience of the American character indexing method and the ease of studying in the United States, as well as the difficulty of Chinese character indexing in China and the inconvenience of studying in China. The reason why it is not difficult to study in the United States is because English words are arranged in order according to the 26 letters of A, B, C, D. It is inconvenient to study in China because China does not have letters and does not have a simple and easy-to-learn character indexing method.

The character indexing method is the foundation of cataloging (Indexscience). Most Chinese students are unwilling to study the subject of cataloging. They do not know that cataloging is the only help for reading and studying. People who understand catalogs can use the library's catalogs to find all relevant books in a library, and use the detailed contents of a book to analyze the essence of the entire book, and be able to find the most things in the shortest amount of time. Without this kind of research, even if you enter the library, you cannot find relevant books without help, and if you have a book in hand, you cannot find the words and things you are looking for without reading it for a long time. The reason why I invented the method of checking Chinese characters is because I had some research on cataloging when I was studying in the United States. I hope that after a simple method is invented, Chinese cataloging will gradually develop, national heritage can be [organized] as soon as possible, and learning methods can be convenient day by day.

The most popular character indexing method in China has always been the radical indexing method. Xu Shen's *Shuo Wen Jie Zi* in the early Han Dynasty and the *Kangxi Dictionary* in the early Qing Dynasty were both compiled successfully based on this method.

The 214 radicals in the *Kangxi Dictionary* are distributed extremely unevenly. The eleven major radicals (人) (mouth 口) (heart 心) (hand 手) (water 水) (wood 木) (gold 金) (grass 艸) (silk 糸) (insect 虫) (speech 言) account for about one-half of the characters in the entire book, while rare radicals (that is, those containing less than twenty characters), such as (人) (口) (卜) (厶), etc., all contain no more than one thousand characters in the 120 divisions and provinces.

The boundaries of the radicals divided in the *Kangxi Dictionary* are extremely unclear. It is clear that the characters of the first radical should belong to the second radical. I don't need to say much about it. As for the number of strokes, which strokes should be connected into one stroke and which should be divided into two strokes, there is no fixed standard. It is very difficult to guess which radical, and you have to calculate the number of strokes. You have to look for the page number of the radical in more than ten or twenty radicals with the same number of strokes, and when you turn to the page number, you have to calculate the number of strokes again. In the same radical and the same number of strokes, among dozens or hundreds of characters (Wang Yunwu said that there are 205 characters with eight strokes in the grass radical and 204 characters with nine strokes in the grass radical), pay attention to each one and search. If you still can't find it, you have to spend twice the effort and wait in one more stroke or one less stroke. If you still can't find it, you have to spend a lot of effort to calculate the total number of strokes of the entire character and look for it among hundreds of characters in the character indexing table (the characters contained in the character indexing table with seven to twelve strokes are all above 200 or 300). In this way, to find the meaning of a small character, you must spend two or three times the effort, go through a long time, count dozens to hundreds of irrelevant characters, and then luckily find the character you are looking for. Do you think it's troublesome? (To be continued)

Laugh It Off 116

— Hai Ke

A: Why did you beat your little brother so hard yesterday?

B: He swallowed a big mouthful of ink. I told him to eat a piece of blotting paper quickly, but he wouldn't.

Music Student: Sir, how do you think my voice is? Will I have any success in the future?

Music Teacher: It couldn't be better for a street vendor selling socks.

A: The other day when you came to my house, my dog bit off a piece of your leg. I'm really sorry.

B: It doesn't matter. I'm a salesman for a department store. I always have to leave some samples wherever I go.

A: I don't think your words match the facts.

B: Are you scolding me for lying?

A: Yes.

B: Then you just scold me straight out for lying. I hate talking in circles.

Botany Professor: When do you think apples should be picked?

A Student: When there are no dogs or gardeners watching in the orchard.

Zhulian Waterfall in Changxing 117

— Ji Jin

The Zhulian Waterfall on Biyan Mountain in Changxing is a famous scenic spot. In the past, when Su Dongpo was the prefect of Wuxing, he would occasionally lead his colleagues to visit. His inscription said, "The Zhulian wants to roll up the rain in the West Mountain, all pouring down towards the Milky Way." This is a factual record. It is a pity that the place is located in a remote rural area and lacks people to care for it, so that the natural beauty has long been submerged in the wilderness. I don't know how many years have passed before it has this fleeting moment of glory today. What are the feelings about this? The following is a brief record of what I learned from a friend's communication.

Changxing is located in a remote mountainous area. There are twelve peaks of Bian, stretching endlessly. Biyan is the highest and largest. The stone walls are thousands of feet high and stand tall in the clouds. The Zhulian water meanders through it. When it reaches the gap, it flows straight down, the momentum is very rapid, and it suddenly becomes a waterfall. It is about thirty feet high. From a distance, it looks like a long white silk hanging from the sky. The sound of gurgling does not stop day and night. The local people often use it to irrigate their fields. Below it is the She Shen Tan. The pool is not wide and flows tortuously to the northeast, passing through Da Dang Yang and entering Taihu Lake. Taihu Lake is a huge pool where all the rivers in western Zhejiang converge. According to research, the distant source of Zhulian water originates from Tianji Ridge on Biyan Mountain, about three miles away. Whenever the Yellow Plum water rises, the momentum becomes more surging. If it cannot be discharged in time, it will spray out from the [missing character] border, and the pearls and jade will splash, making it even more spectacular. The most peculiar thing is that when there is no rain for a long time and it becomes a drought, this water will never run dry due to the exhaustion of the flow. Some say that the Tianji spring source is connected to Tianmu, which is credible. It is now heard that the Bianxiang district committee of this county has been ordered to investigate and is urgently constructing it. If it can be renewed and expanded, then the scenery of western Zhejiang will definitely add a lot of color to the lakes and mountains.

News from the Bandit Suppression in Northern Jiangsu 118

— Qi

The area around Tongzhou and Rugao in northern Jiangsu has always been known for its peace. However, in recent years, banditry has become rampant, causing unrest among the local people. What follows is a description of what I have heard and seen, written for this publication.

Self-Defense Eradicates Bandits: In a certain town in the eastern part of Tongzhou, there was a clan of the surname "Mou" living together. All the clan members were wealthy, with some possessing tens of thousands of gold and others up to hundreds of thousands. Recognizing the ferocity of the bandits and their repeated covetousness, they joined forces to devise a plan to defend against them. On one hand, they built defensive fortifications, and on the other hand, they procured firearms, amassing considerable strength, including handheld machine guns and searchlights. One night, a patrolman used a searchlight on a lookout tower and saw dark shadows looming several miles away, like a swarm of ants, rushing towards them with great force. He fired a volley of shots into the sky, but the rushing continued unabated. He then fired into the crowd, but still to no avail, and they drew closer and closer. When they were not far from the houses, he fired the machine gun, and the bandits finally retreated. Upon inspecting the scene, he found more than ninety people shot down, mostly tenant farmers and neighbors, holding farming tools in their hands. When asked, those who were not dead claimed that they had been coerced by the communists and would be shot if they disobeyed. The bandits were at the rear, and anyone who retreated would be killed. Therefore, these people advanced to their deaths, and retreating meant death as well, leaving them with no other choice.

Failed Joint Suppression: The town of Taoxiang in Rugao, bordering Tongzhou, was a den of communist bandits. After the area was captured by the bandits, government troops did not arrive for several months, allowing the bandits to occupy it. The administrative and public security bureaus were all destroyed, and the problem grew, becoming a major threat to the Pingchao area of Tongzhou. Chen Buchan, the magistrate of Nantong County, known for his bandit suppression efforts, seeing the plight of the people, invited the magistrate of Rugao County to join him in suppressing the bandits. At midnight on the appointed day, the troops of Tongzhou were mobilized and launched a courageous siege. However, the magistrate of Rugao County broke his promise. Thus, they could only watch as the communist bandit leaders leisurely escaped towards the border, missing a golden opportunity.

It is truly regrettable, and the soldiers and police of Tongzhou were particularly indignant. If they had been defeated by the bandits, and the reinforcements from Rugao had not arrived, would it not have meant total annihilation? It is now reported that the local authorities have lodged a serious protest with the Rugao government.

Beheading for Public Display: After a successful bandit suppression campaign, the head of a bandit was hung up for public display to appease the people and intimidate the bandits. On the eleventh, it was brought to Pingchao Town and displayed on a stone pillar at a crossroads. A crowd immediately gathered to watch. The bandit's face was as yellow as gold paper, and he did not look particularly frightening. I sighed and said, "He was once a hero, but where is he now?" Human beings slaughter each other, and the killing intent is greatly unleashed. Although the bandit's death is deserved, the changes in the world are truly lamentable.

An On-the-Spot Examination 119

— Lan Yin

In recent years, many divorce cases have occurred in Peixian, accompanied by various farcical events. Such a phenomenon is quite unusual for an inland area. The most notable case is that of Zhang Biyue, which caused a nationwide sensation. Biyue divorced a man surnamed Wu, and her sister divorced a man surnamed Hao, leading to the tragic shooting of Huang Changdian. The incident was even adapted into a new play in Shanghai. I believe readers may still remember it. Recently, another amusing story of an on-the-spot examination occurred, similar to the "dissecting the abdomen to verify the flower" incident. Fortunately, the county magistrate acted as a Lou Lian, using kind words to mediate, and the couple was able to reconcile. Initially, there was a man surnamed Mou who was quite unattractive. He had graduated from middle school and was therefore quite knowledgeable. He was the opposite of those who are outwardly beautiful but inwardly flawed. His wife was beautiful and intelligent, but they had been married for three years and had not yet had children. She was unhappy with her husband's unattractive appearance. Quarrels were often heard outside their home. They were husband and wife in name only, without the happiness of a couple, and she had long intended to divorce. Under the influence of the new trends, her determination grew stronger. Finally, they quarreled over an incident and went to the county government, requesting a divorce. The county magistrate summoned Mou and asked if he wanted a divorce. He said he did, but that his wife was pregnant with his child, which should be returned to him. His wife glared at him and said, "I am not pregnant. He is deliberately making things difficult." She then bared her abdomen to the county magistrate and said, "It is not difficult to know whether I am pregnant or not with a single touch." The county magistrate was very embarrassed. Mou insisted on his previous statement, saying, "The pregnancy is still in its early stages and cannot be seen from the outside. How can it be known with a single touch?" The wife became very angry and said in a stern voice, "Then please let the county magistrate dissect me to find out the truth!" As she spoke, she held up her bare abdomen, demanding an immediate dissection. At this point, the county magistrate realized that Mou still did not want to divorce, so he changed his expression and began to persuade and comfort them. His wife also realized that dissecting her abdomen to verify the pregnancy was a matter of life and death, and she became slightly discouraged. Shame and aversion also took hold of her, and she bowed her head and returned home with her husband.

Table Treasures Record 120

— Zheng Yimei

Last night, Mr. Zhao Lantang hosted a banquet at the Jue Lin Temple. Yimei also attended the grand occasion. In the midst of the bustling crowd, I had the pleasure of meeting Mr. Yao Yuping, a revolutionary veteran. Mr. Yao had a thin face and a slight mustache. His hair was already gray, and he spoke gently and kindly. He is now a resident of Shanghai, living in seclusion and refusing guests, not concerning himself with the state of affairs. He is devoted to Zen meditation, sitting in silence all day, saying, "All truths can be realized through meditation. Otherwise, chanting scriptures and reciting Buddhist texts is merely a formality." These are truly wise words. The Jue Lin Temple did not have wine, but Mr. Luo Liangong cannot be happy without a cup. He specially ordered a servant to buy some. In his drunkenness, he recounted a time when he drank at someone's house, tasting forty-year-old aged wine. The taste was light, harmonious, and mellow. He unknowingly emptied his cup again and again. The host repeatedly stopped him, saying, "Aged wine should not be drunk in excess, lest you become intoxicated." At the time, I thought the host was being stingy, not allowing me to drink to my fill. But when I left, a cool breeze blew on me, and my eyes were blurred and my head was dizzy. I could hardly stand. Only then did I realize the power of aged wine. No wonder the host repeatedly stopped me. A certain gentleman at the table then mentioned that his family had lychee wine. In the past, Wang Shipeng ate lychees and wrote the line, "How dare I eat the 'Jade Hall Red'?" So he adopted the beautiful name "Jade Hall Red." In midsummer, he peels fresh lychees and puts them into sorghum wine, adding Xiangtang rock sugar, and then seals it tightly, away from the wind and sun. After ten years, it ferments and can be drunk. Its color is crimson, its taste sweet, fragrant, and rich, and it has the effect of strengthening the stomach. It is not available on the market. Mr. Qian Huahuo immediately requested a jar, hoping to share it with his friends one day, so that they could all enjoy the taste of this exquisite nectar.

Tea Addiction 121

— Wenzhong

In recent years, Shanghai literati have formed poetry societies to write and harmonize with each other. Mr. Chen Zhuzun and Mr. Liang Yantian are both members of the society. One is known for his drinking capacity, and the other for his tea addiction. Mr. Zhuzun's drinking capacity has already been recorded in this publication by Wan Chengjun. Today, I will talk about Mr. Yantian's tea addiction.

Mr. Yantian is an old classicist, over seventy years old, but his spirit is vigorous and he walks faster than a young man. He is extremely fond of tea. In his room, besides the zither and books, there is a tea set on his desk. When the mood strikes, he brews tea himself, holding a cup in his left hand and a brush in his right, drinking and chanting poetry all day long. He says, "Reciting poetry without drinking tea is dry and tasteless, and inspiration does not arise." His poem says: "Every time I encounter fine wine, my heart is drunk first; I love to brew new tea myself. How many days have I returned to my hometown with a cane? Joining the society with a group of virtuous people." From this, one can see a glimpse. (Thank you)

European Travel Correspondence (41) 122

— Liu Haisu

▲ The Death of Putaier

(2) Funeral

The next day, the weather was dark and gloomy in the morning, threatening rain. It was very depressing. Around two o'clock in the afternoon, yellow fog rose up in the sky, as if mourning the death of this great sculptor. After three o'clock, Ms. Xiao, Peng Shiqin, Chuan Lei, and Zhang Xuan gathered at my studio at 20 Rue de la Sorbonne. We then took motorcycles to Impasse du Marne. This was not only to pay our respects to the remains of this great figure, but also to see many of the master's unpublished masterpieces.

"Hero worship" is a common human psychology, especially my own peculiar habit. Therefore, I do not shy away from my "close contact with great figures." This time, I came to Europe to study and also wanted to pay my respects to a few heroes. The painters Henri Matisse, Pablo Picasso, Antler Duran, and Feng Na; the poet Valery; the literary giant Romain Rolland; and the sculptor Antoine Putaier were all on my list to meet. Now, before I could meet Putaier, he suddenly died. How saddened I was.

As the car sped through the city streets, it was pouring rain. This made me feel even more desolate. Turning right on the main road, there was a row of short, slightly brownish-yellow walls, clinging to old vines that ran horizontally and vertically. It was truly ancient and desolate. Four police officers stood in front of the gate. Many people were coming and going. Our car also stopped. Mr. Chuan went up, took off his hat, and asked, "Is Mr. Putaier's L'atelier here?"

One of them, with white whiskers and a tall figure, replied, "This is it."

Walking into the courtyard, the large trees seemed unable to withstand the wind and frost, and yellow withered leaves fell on our heads. After walking dozens of steps further, on the left, there was a tall, black building with glass windows. It looked like it had been exposed to the wind and rain for twenty or thirty years. This was the famous Putaier's L'atelier. Looking at the long row of glass windows, I thought to myself, Putaier constantly created many immortal and magical masterpieces, probably in that room.

As it was raining, it was as dark as dusk. The L'atelier was lit with bright electric lights. Many people had come to participate in the funeral. We stood outside the door in the downpour. Two masters of ceremonies, dressed in black formal attire, wearing thick silver chains around their necks, with red faces full of pimples, and golden-yellow hair and beards, were very eye-catching. They respectfully asked the guests to sign their names one by one and entered the door in a solemn and reverent manner. In the center was placed Putaier's remains. Countless flowers were piled all around, especially the wreaths in the back, which were piled as high as the roof. Two three-foot-long white candles were placed on either side of the remains. The dim candlelight flickered in the wind, revealing a mournful and sorrowful color. In the corner on the left, a statue of Rodin was placed high up. To commemorate his teacher, Auguste Rodin, Putaier created this statue of the great artist. The thoughtful eyes and the vigorous and broad forehead shone with magical charm. The spirit of a deeply thoughtful and sublime artist was expressed here. It can be said to be a very bold and symbolic representation of the whole person of Rodin. It seemed as if he was right in front of you. Below it was also carved "My Teacher Rodin." On the left was a twenty-foot-high and eight-foot-wide relief sculpture, an unfinished large-scale concept. The large work in front was a completely gigantic illusion. The left hand was stretched straight out, and the muscles of the whole body were tense like a lion roaring. It had the face of a Babylonian or Assyrian grotesque giant statue. It was truly a bold attempt. There were also many of his recent works all around. Because it was a solemn funeral, we could not look at each one in detail. Mrs. Putaier and other relatives were all wearing black mourning clothes, sitting on one side of the remains. Most of the guests stood solemnly around, taking turns to pay their respects and瞻仰遺容. I also ran forward to瞻仰瞻仰. His face looked like a triangle at first glance. The top of his head was completely bald. His forehead was broad and protruding. On both sides of his temples, there were patches of white hair that connected to the beard on his chin. His cheekbones were very wide. His eyes were deep and sunken, as if he were asleep. His mouth was tightly closed. Although he was dead, his face still showed a clear, deep, and radiant demeanor.

Before long, more and more mourners gathered. An old man in his eighties came in and burst into tears. He said that he had received a letter from him ten days ago. He learned of the sad news yesterday morning and came to Paris specially. Now he was saying goodbye to him forever. Many people comforted him and helped him to sit with Mrs. Putaier. He was still crying uncontrollably. The room was silent and even more solemn and desolate.

Strangely enough, we stood there for an hour and did not want to leave the L'atelier. Later, there were too many people, and we could not stay any longer. I looked back again and again and left the room.

Gold Market is Greatly Weakened After the Swap 125

The initial peak continued to decline, with the price slightly weakening by 0.25 taels. Yesterday, the gold market was again in a weak state. However, the initial peak occurred in the afternoon, with the morning market estimated at 7 taels difference. The afternoon market was also estimated to fluctuate around 3 taels and several qian. The market atmosphere was chaotic. Some dealers were quick to buy and sell, but supply and demand differed. Yuan Sheng, Sheng Da, Yuan Mao Yong, Da De Cheng, Shun Li, and others bought in, while some major players shorted and sold off positions, such as Yong Heng, Yu Da, Zhi Feng Yong, and Tai Xing. As for the exchange rate, it had already been reduced by one level, but the internal trend was weakening rather than strengthening. Some dealers were selling. The early market was strong, and the price once rose to over 493 taels. Later, major players sold off, and the exchange rate also turned to a deficit trend, resulting in a continuous decline of as much as 5 taels. In the initial stages of the afternoon market, it was still stable. Later, Japanese banks and speculators sold off in droves, and foreign exchange deteriorated, with each pound sterling worth 2 shillings. It fell by more than 3 taels and broke through 85 taels. Later, various parties made some purchases, and the situation eased, rebounding by 1-2 taels, but there were ups and downs from time to time, while foreign exchange was flat. Transactions were smooth. The final price was 86 taels and zero qian, a decrease of 3 taels and 9 qian from the previous day's closing price. In general, the investors were in a chaotic mood, and the price fluctuated in a narrow range. Yesterday was the beginning of the week, and there was no telegraphic news from the major regulations.

In the early morning, major players bought heavily and opened at a high price. The opening price for the April gold standard was 491 taels and 2 qian, an increase of 1 tael. Later, it rose to 93 taels and 4 qian, probably because major players were buying heavily. The exchange rate was also strong. The Japanese gold price was 1 tael and 0.025 by Sumitomo. The British gold price was 11 pence and 6875 by the British and Indian merchants. However, the gross price fell back by more than 2 taels due to the major players selling off. Therefore, when the ordinance was announced, it was 91 taels. Subsequently, there were slight increases and decreases. Yarn and Cotton Demand Unenthusiastic, Yarn Market Flat and Weary 129

The cotton yarn market is flat and weary, because the overseas yarn market is trending downward again, and actual

sales have not been stimulated. The inventory is not easily eliminated in a short time, and people's confidence is relatively weak. The prosperity or decline of current actual sales directly dominates the advance and retreat of the yarn market. The spring sales season is approaching, but customer groups do not seem very enthusiastic. Although there are daily transactions of one or two thousand bales, the public believes that this sales volume is considered smooth in the off-season, but it is not considered satisfactory during this period. Further analysis of the yarn inventory shows that the number of coarse yarns exceeds that of fine count yarns, which is why people's confidence cannot be aroused for the time being. According to inquiries, customer groups have the following concerns: First, the agricultural situation in the interior is not ideal, and purchasing power is weak. Second, changes in current events and bandit disasters cause frequent traffic disruptions. Therefore, the intention to purchase is not strong. However, in the futures yarn market, the buyers are all large households, while the sellers are all retail investors. Therefore, although people's confidence is weak, the market presents a situation of hesitation. What the future holds depends solely on actual sales.

Futures yarn fell seven qian. People in the exchange mark standard yarn. The morning market was initially quite firm, but then actual sales were sluggish, the third grade trended downward, and the market turned weary. Each month rose and fell by two, three, or four qian. In the afternoon, the third grade reported a decline, people's confidence was weaker, and the market continued to be weary. Each month fell by three qian to seven qian. The total transaction volume was 14,300 bales. The closing price of the standard yarn is recorded below:

Marked Flour Market Turns Soft 136

Silk and Tea, Difficulty in Implementing Baking Tests for Anhui and Hubei Coarse Silk 137

The yellow and white coarse silk produced in Anhui and Hubei provinces is sold extensively in England and France. Because the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau is scheduled to implement inspection and testing of exported Chinese silk on March 1, if the Anhui and Hubei yellow and white silk are subjected to baking tests, the color of the silk will inevitably change and the silk threads will become brittle, which does not meet the needs of Europe and America. It will inevitably be ignored and difficult to comply with. Representatives have now been elected to petition for exemption from inspection.

Seafood, Kelp Arrival is Scarce, Market Rises 140

The production price of kelp is gradually rising, which is the opposite of the Shanghai market trend. Therefore, the firms have tightened their hands on goods and are generally unwilling to sell them. Moreover, the inventory of each shop has long been exhausted, and the source of production goods has long been lacking due to the relationship between the expensive price. As a result, customers often need to prepare for a shortage of goods on the market, so the market is also rising step by step. The day before yesterday, traders who were hawking already shouted for price increases. Shanghai Municipal Bank 141

Grand Opening Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Bank held its opening ceremony at 9:00 a.m. yesterday. The grand occasion is described in detail below:

Opening Ceremony: At 8:40 a.m., the clock rang. First, General Manager Xu Shengchan, Manager Gu Yinong, Deputy Manager Chen Zhangwen, and all staff members performed a meeting ceremony. Next, the Deputy Manager performed the opening ceremony. Then, the General Manager gave a training speech to all the staff, stating that the main purpose of the establishment of the Shanghai Municipal Bank was to (1) concentrate the city's wealth, (2) unify the city's income and expenditure, (3) adjust the city's finances, and (4) develop the city's business. Therefore, all countries attach great importance to municipal banks. China did not have one before. The Capital Special Municipality was established the year before last. This bank is actually the second. Now it is in the germination stage. Although the funds are only 1 million yuan, since this bank holds the general hub of the city's finances, there is no end to its future business. Even if only the income and expenditure of the municipal government are counted, the annual amount is already very large. In addition, with the various exchanges of industry and commerce and the public, as well as the various equipment for the city's business, the development of the future has no limits. I encourage you all, etc.

Guests: Those who attended included Zhang Yongni, Vice Minister of Finance; Zhang Xiqing, Lianghuai Salt Transport Envoy; Ren Guangyu, Chief of Staff of the Naval Headquarters; Chen Xunyong, Fleet Commander; Yin Yinong, former Director of the Navigation Administration Department of the Ministry of Communications; Zhu Shoumei, Director of the Management Department of the Headquarters; Wu Qiding, Director of the Jiangsu Shatian Official Property Affairs Bureau; Wang Yiting, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Qian'an, Lu Jianquan, Li Fuxun, Tang Shoumin, Bei Songsun, Xie Hengchuang, Ye Kuichu, Xu Jiqing, Wu Zhihao, Yuan Lidun, Zhu Chengzhang, Shen Lianfang, Zhou Peizhen, Lu Daizhi, the Director of the Secretariat of the Municipal Government Council, and the heads of various bureaus, as well as important staff members from various banks and companies, totaling more than 1,000 people.

Meeting: At 9:00 a.m., the clock rang nine times, announcing the start of the meeting. The meeting was presided over by Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Special Municipal Government Council Bureau, representing Mayor Zhang. (1) Playing music to open the bank, (2) Chairman, representatives of various agencies, and all participating guests and staff members take their seats, (3) bowing three times to the national flag and party flag, (4) Chairman respectfully reads the President's will, (5) three minutes of silence, (6) directors, supervisors, general manager, and deputy general manager swear to take office, (7) guests deliver congratulatory speeches, (8) chairman's reply, (9) completion of the ceremony and playing of music, (10) tea and refreshments.

Speeches: First, Xu Jiqing delivered a congratulatory speech on behalf of the guests, saying, "To promote the development of industry and commerce and the advancement of culture in a city, it is necessary to first improve the municipal administration and engage in construction, and finance is the general hub. The Shanghai Municipal Government used to be corrupt and never considered construction, so there was no special bank. Since General Zhang Gongyue took over the municipal government, the establishment of a municipal bank was planned. Since Xu Gongshengchan has been in charge of the Finance Bureau, the municipal bank has been realized. The municipal bank manages the city's finances, so it assists in municipal construction and protects the welfare of the public. Its mission is significant and cannot be compared to ordinary financial institutions. After months of preparation, the business plan has been successfully completed. In the future, we will see the spread of grand plans, the promotion of the city's civilization, and the realization of the plan for a Greater Shanghai. Its reputation will be known throughout the country. It will be more than just a bank for the citizens. Today, on the grand opening ceremony, I respectfully offer these humble words to express my congratulations." Next, Xie Hengchuang, Chu Minyi, and others gave speeches one after another, saying that the municipal bank assists in the construction of the municipal administration and promotes the development of municipal business, which benefits all citizens and the public. We know that it will definitely thrive in the future, and the greatness of the future can be predicted.
